 Natural language question: How many years did the second oldest dog in the world live?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT ?result WHERE{?dog wdt:P31 wd:Q144. ?dog wdt:P569 ?db; wdt:P570 ?dd BIND((YEAR(?dd) - YEAR(?db)) AS ?result)} ORDER BY DESC(?result) LIMIT 1 OFFSET 1
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?yearsLived WHERE {
  ?dog wdt:P31 wd:Q144.  # instance of dog
  ?dog wdt:P569 ?birthDate.
  ?dog wdt:P570 ?deathDate.
  BIND(YEAR(?deathDate) - YEAR(?birthDate) AS ?yearsLived)
}
ORDER BY DESC(?yearsLived)
LIMIT 1
OFFSET 1  # for second oldest
```

    }

}

PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT (SUM(?rev) AS ?result) WHERE {{SELECT DISTINCT ?company WHERE {?company wdt:P361 wd:Q30748112. ?company wdt:P1128 ?num} ORDER BY DESC(?num) LIMIT 3} ?company p:P2139 ?ps. ?ps ps:P2139 ?rev; pq:P585 ?time. FILTER(NOT EXISTS{?company p:P2139/pq:P585 ?time2 FILTER(?time2 > ?time)})}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT (SUM(?revenue) AS ?totalRevenue)
WHERE {
  wd:Q30748112 wdt:P361 ?bigTechCompany .
  ?bigTechCompany wdt:P1128 ?numEmployees .
  ?bigTechCompany p:P2139 ?revenueStatement .
  ?revenueStatement ps:P2139 ?revenue .
  ?revenueStatement pq:P585 ?date .
  FILTER(YEAR(?date) = 2022)
}
ORDER BY DESC(?numEmployees)
LIMIT 3
```

 Natural language question: Which archipelago has more islands: the Galápagos Islands or the Hawaiian Islands ?

  ?island wdt:P31 wd:Q192626.
}
GROUP BY ?archipelago
ORDER BY DESC(?numberOfIslands)

} ORDER BY ?inceptionDate LIMIT 1

QueryNumber: 298
 Natural language question: Did Germany have a population growth of at least 1% since 2010?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> ASK {wd:Q183 p:P1082 ?ps10, ?psNew. ?ps10 pq:P585 ?t10; ps:P1082 ?p10. ?psNew pq:P585 ?tNew; ps:P1082 ?pNew BIND(((?pNew - ?p10) / ?p10) AS ?diff) FILTER((YEAR(?t10) = 2010) && NOT EXISTS{wd:Q183 p:P1082/pq:P585 ?tt FILTER(?tt > ?tNew)} && ?diff >= 0.01)}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
ASK {
  {
    SELECT (MAX(?population2010) as ?maxPopulation2010) {
      wd:Q183 p:P1082 ?popStatement2010.
      ?popStatement2010 ps:P1082 ?population2010.
      ?popStatement2010 pq:P585 ?date2010.
      FILTER(YEAR(?date2010) = 2010)
    }
  }
  {
    SELECT (MAX(?populationRecent) as ?maxPopulationRecent) {
      wd:Q183 p:P1082 ?popStatementRecent.
      ?popStatementRecent ps:P1082 ?populationRecent.
      ?popStatementRecent pq:P585 ?dateRecent.
      FILTER(YEAR(?dateRecent) >= 2010)
    }
  }
  BIND((?maxPopulationRecent - ?maxPopulation2010) / ?maxPopulation2010 * 100 AS ?growthPercentage)
  FILTER(?growthPercentage >= 1)
}
```

QueryNumber: 311
 Natural language question: Which NBA teams have won the most seasons?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT DISTINCT ?result WHERE {{SELECT DISTINCT (COUNT(DISTINCT ?season) AS ?max) WHERE {?season wdt:P31 wd:Q27020041; wdt:P3450 wd:Q155223; wdt:P1346 ?result. ?result wdt:P31 wd:Q13393265} GROUP BY ?result ORDER BY DESC (?max) LIMIT 1} ?season wdt:P31 wd:Q27020041; wdt:P3450 wd:Q155223; wdt:P1346 ?result. ?result wdt:P31 wd:Q13393265.} GROUP BY ?result HAVING ((COUNT(DISTINCT ?season)) = MAX(?max))
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?team (COUNT(?season) AS ?number_of_seasons_won)
WHERE {
  ?team wdt:P31 wd:Q155223.
  ?team wdt:P1346 ?season.
  ?season wdt:P3450 wd:Q27020041.
}
GROUP BY ?team
ORDER BY DESC(?number_of_seasons_won)
LIMIT 10
```

QueryNumber: 344
 Natural language question: Who was an actor in more movies, Daniel Day Lewis or Paul Dano ?
 Correct SPARQL query: 
PREFIX bd: <http://www.bigdata.com/rdf#> PREFIX dct: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/> PREFIX geo: <http://www.opengis.net/ont/geosparql#> PREFIX p: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/> PREFIX pq: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/qualifier/> PREFIX ps: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/> PREFIX psn: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/statement/value-normalized/> PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> PREFIX wd: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/> PREFIX wds: <http://www.wikidata.org/entity/statement/> PREFIX wdt: <http://www.wikidata.org/prop/direct/> PREFIX wdv: <http://www.wikidata.org/value/> PREFIX wikibase: <http://wikiba.se/ontology#> PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> SELECT DISTINCT ?result WHERE {{SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?film) AS ?ddl) WHERE {?film wdt:P161 wd:Q166389; wdt:P31 wd:Q11424}} {SELECT (COUNT (DISTINCT ?film) AS ?pd) WHERE {?film wdt:P161 wd:Q343616; wdt:P31 wd:Q11424}} BIND(IF((?ddl > ?pd), wd:Q166389, wd:Q343616) AS ?result)}
 Generated sparql query: 
```sparql
SELECT ?danielCount ?paulCount WHERE {
  {
    SELECT (COUNT(?film1) AS ?danielCount) WHERE {
      ?film1 wdt:P161 wd:Q343616 .
      ?film1 wdt:P31 wd:Q11424 .
    }
  }
  {
    SELECT (COUNT(?film2) AS ?paulCount) WHERE {
      ?film2 wdt:P161 wd:Q166389 .
      ?film2 wdt:P31 wd:Q11424 .
    }
  }
  BIND(?danielCount > ?paulCount AS ?danielMore)
}
```
 Recall: 0.0
 Accuracy: 0
 Precision: 0.0
 Query error LLM: False
 Query error dataset: False
